<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // Click event listener for pricing table buttons
    $(document).on('click', '.elementor-price-table .elementor-button', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Get the heading text of the clicked pricing table and trim whitespace
        var headingText = $(this).closest('.elementor-price-table').find('.elementor-price-table__heading').text().trim();

        // Set the heading text to the form field after a short delay
        setTimeout(function() {
            var displayField = $('#form-field-idtarget'); // Replace with your actual form field ID
            if (displayField.length) {
                displayField.val(''); // Clear the field first
                displayField.val(headingText).prop('readonly', true);
            }
        }, 500);
    });
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  var starfield = document.getElementById('starfield');
  var stars = 20;

  for (var i = 0; i < stars; i++) {
    var star = document.createElement('div');
    star.className = 'star';
    starfield.appendChild(star);

    star.style.left = Math.random() * 100 + '%';
    star.style.top = Math.random() * 100 + '%';

    (function(star) {
      var speedX = (Math.random() - 0.9) * 0.09;
      var speedY = (Math.random() - 0.9) * 0.09;

      function move() {
        var left = parseFloat(star.style.left);
        var top = parseFloat(star.style.top);
        
        left += speedX;
        top += speedY;

        if (left > 100 || left < 0) {
          speedX *= -1;
        }
        if (top > 100 || top < 0) {
          speedY *= -1;
        }

        star.style.left = left + '%';
        star.style.top = top + '%';
        requestAnimationFrame(move);
      }
      move();
    })(star);
  }
});
</script>


<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  var stars = document.querySelectorAll('.star');
  
  stars.forEach(function(star) {
    var randomDelay = Math.random() * 5;
    star.style.animationDelay = randomDelay + 's';
  });
});
</script>

								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );

						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
